batik-javadoc in fedora-33

This page displays detail informations of the batik-javadoc package. You might want go back to the main page of batik-javadoc.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-08-18 Mat Booth - 1.13-1 - Update to latest upstream release - Add requirements on full JRE for subpackages that require AWT
2020-07-27 Fedora Release Engineering - 1.11-7 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_33_Mass_Rebuild
2020-07-10 Jiri Vanek - 1.11-6 - Rebuilt for JDK-11, see https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Changes/Java11
2020-06-15 Fedora Release Engineering - 1.11-4 - build with --xmvn-javadoc
2020-01-28 Fedora Release Engineering - 1.11-3 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2019-07-24 Fedora Release Engineering - 1.11-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_31_Mass_Rebuild
2019-05-15 Mat Booth - 1.11-1 - Update to latest upstream release - Drop ancient obsoletes - Drop eclipse-specific hacks that are no longer needed - Allow conditional building without scripting engines for smaller dep chain - Break out some low-level modules into separate sub-package for smaller install size
2019-01-31 Fedora Release Engineering - 1.10-4 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_30_Mass_Rebuild
2018-08-30 Severin Gehwolf - 1.10-3 - Add explicit javapackages-tools requirement for sub-packages using jpackage_script-based scripts. See RHBZ#1600426.
